<section class="propertydetails">
<div class="propertydetails-description">
<div class="propertydetails-section_title">Property Description:</div>
<div>This gorgeous house sits on large 42' x 122' lot in Arbutus. Supreme finishing &amp; craftsmanship throughout. Designed to provide best contemporary living space of over 3600 SF, including granite tile &amp; hardwood flooring thru-out, kitchen w/ top-of-the-line appliances &amp; custom cabinetry. 3 ensuited bdrms upstairs. entertainment recreation room w/ wet bar, steam shower / sauna room, 2 bdrms &amp; media room in basement. Features: smart home system, A/C, HRV, secured fenced yard , 3-car garage etc. Just walk steps to Carnarvon Elementary, park &amp; transit. Easy access to Arbutus shopping, W 4th &amp; Broadway shopping street, UBC &amp; much more. Schools nearby: Prince of Wales Sec., Trafalgar Elem., York House, Little Flower Academy etc.</div>
</div>
